  14: data = NW2016_dataset
  15: data = data[data.isna()['psl'] == False]
  16: #Drop useless columns
  17: data = data.drop(columns = ['lat', 'lon', 'height_sta'], axis = 1)
  18: 
  19: data['date'] = pd.to_datetime(data['date'], format='%Y%m%d %H:%M')
  20: data.set_index('date', inplace=True)
  21: 
  22: #Interpolate missing values
  23: data = data.interpolate(method='linear')
  24: 
  25: stats = data.describe()
  26: stats = stats.transpose()
  27: data = normalize(data, stats)
  28: resample_ds = data.resample(TIMESTEP).mean()
  29: 
  30: train_ds = resample_ds.sample(frac=0.7)
  31: test_ds = resample_ds.drop(train_ds.index)
  32: 
  33: X_train, y_train = segment(train_ds, "td", window = HISTORY_LAG, future = FUTURE_TARGET)
  34: X_train = X_train.reshape(X_train.shape[0], HISTORY_LAG, 1)
  35: y_train = y_train.reshape(y_train.shape[0], FUTURE_TARGET, 1)
  36: 
  37: X_test, y_test = segment(train_ds, "td", window = HISTORY_LAG, future = FUTURE_TARGET)
  38: X_test = X_test.reshape(X_test.shape[0], HISTORY_LAG, 1)
  39: y_test = y_test.reshape(y_test.shape[0], FUTURE_TARGET,)
  40: 
  41: print(len(X_train), 'train sequences')
  42: print(len(X_test), 'test sequences')
